The Chinese Legal Education Association's First Annual Meeting Concludes

Passing Recommendations on National Crisis Education to be Sent to Various Schools for Implementation

Electing Committee Members to Study Various Specialized Issues in Groups

Central University, Daxia University, and Shanghai Law College Serve as Host Schools This Year

The Chinese Legal Education Association, organized by law faculties and departments nationwide, continued to hold its first annual meeting at the YMCA on Ba Xian Qiao yesterday. Proposals were discussed in the morning, the Lawyers Association hosted a luncheon at noon, Zhang Yaozeng and others gave speeches in the afternoon, and association affairs were discussed. The meeting concluded at around 7 PM. Details are recorded below:

Representatives from Various Schools Attending: Included Dongwu's Yang Yongqing, Sheng Zhenwei, Sun Xiaolou, Yu Chengxiu; Fudan's Li Denghui, Jin Tongyin, Zhang Zhirang; Daxia's Sun Gao, Zhang Junqing; Shanghai Law College's Shen Junru, Pan Dada; Fujian College's Huang Puxin; Xiamen's Zhang Qingzhen; Aurora's Lou Ying, Shan Yuhua, Ge Zhiqin, Gu Shouxi; Chizhi's Shi Lin, Zhou Dingmei; Chaoyang's Chen Zhenlu; Zhonggong's Wu Jie, and over twenty other people.

Discussion on National Crisis Education: Chairman Yang Yongqing discussed the following proposals: In order to facilitate research on specialized issues in legal education, this association will organize separate groups for A. Curriculum Design, B. Legal Education Materials, C. Legal Theory Teaching, D. Commemoration of Deceased Legal Scholars, E. Publications, F. Comparative Law. Each group will have five to nine members, elected at the annual meeting, and one member will be elected from among the members to be responsible for convening the group and reporting at the next annual meeting. The resolution was passed. Regarding the research on legal aspects of the war and the proposal to add courses related to law and war in law departments to meet the purpose of national crisis education, the resolution was passed in principle and the original proposers were entrusted to revise it according to the opinions of the meeting and submit it to the association for forwarding to the schools for consideration and implementation, and also for reference by the curriculum group. The proposal to organize a series of lectures on legal education was passed. The proposal to enrich legal education and the proposal that law schools should focus on theoretical subjects and add practical subjects were resolved to be handled in the same way as the first proposal. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Lawyers Association Luncheon: At noon, the Shanghai Lawyers Association hosted a luncheon for all members at the YMCA on Ba Xian Qiao. Lu Dingkui, a standing committee member of the Lawyers Association, gave a welcoming speech, and Yang Yongqing and Huang Puxin of the Legal Education Association gave thank-you speeches. The banquet ended at around 2 PM.

Electing Members of Various Groups: The meeting continued after 2 PM to discuss the selection of members for various groups. The following were approved: Comparative Law Group: Wu Jingxiong, Li Pu, Zhang Qingzhen, Zhang Shouchang, Ning Baiqing, Zhang Junqing, Zai Hanzhang, Liu Shifang, etc. Curriculum Design Group: Sheng Zhenwei, Zhou Xinmin, Wang Jin, Ge Zhiqin, Wu Jie, Shen Junru, Sun Xiaolou, etc. Publications Group: Li Zuyin, Pan Dada, Wang Furu, Xue Zuguang, Sun Xiaolou, Wang Shaotang, Yu Chengxiu, etc. Commemoration of Deceased Legal Scholars Group: Shen Junru, Zeng Yuchun, Wang Xiaotong, Zhu Zhangbao, etc. Legal Theory Guidance Group: Yang Yongqing, Xie Jingshan, Zhang Zhirang, Lou Ying, Yang De'en, Zhou Dingmei, Shan Yuhua, etc. Legal Education Materials Group: Shi Lin, Wang Qufei, Lei Guoneng, Jin Lansun, etc.

Location of the Next Annual Meeting: Finally, the issue of the date and location of the second annual meeting was discussed. It was resolved that the location would be Nanjing and the date would be during the summer vacation this year. As for the host schools for this session, Central University in Nanjing, Daxia University in Shanghai, and Fujian Law College were elected on the spot. After the discussion, former Minister of Justice Zhang Yaozeng and others were invited to give academic speeches on the topic of Social Life and Its Development. Their arguments were precise and appropriate. Dongwu Law School specially dispatched students to record the speeches, which lasted for about an hour. By the time the meeting adjourned, the city was lit up with lights.

Survey of Law Schools Nationwide: The association conducted separate surveys of universities and independent colleges with law departments in the country during the preparatory period. The following is published for reference: (A) Universities: Central University Law School, President Luo Jialun (Nanjing); Zhongshan University Law School, President Zou Lu (Guangzhou); Peiping University Law and Commerce School, President Xu Songming (Peiping); Peking University Law School, President Jiang Menglin (Peiping); Tsinghua University Law School, President Mei Yiqi (Peiping); Wuhan University Law School, President Wang Xinggong (Wuchang); Sichuan University Law School, President Ren Hongjun (Chengdu); Above are National Universities. Henan University Law School, President Yang Zhenwen (Kaifeng); Shanxi University Law School, President Wang Luxun (Taiyuan); Yunnan University College of Arts and Law, President He Yao (Kunming); Northeastern University Law School, President Wang Zhuoran (Peiping); Jilin University College of Arts and Law, President (Unknown) (Jilin). Above are Provincial Universities. Guangdong National University Law School, President Wu Dingxin (Guangzhou); Guangzhou University Law School, President Jin Zengcheng (Guangzhou); Daxia University Law School, President Wang Boqun (Shanghai); Fudan University Law School, President Li Denghui (Shanghai); Dongwu University Law School, President Yang Yongqing (Shanghai); Aurora University Law School, President Hu Wenyao (Shanghai); Yenching University Law School, President Zhou Yichun (Peiping); Wuchang University College of Arts (with Law Courses), President Chen Shi (Wuchang); Xiamen University College of Law and Commerce, President Lin Wenqing (Xiamen). One director has been appointed for each of the senior high and junior high departments, Xu Chun, a mathematics and physics assistant teacher from Guanghua University, and Fang Ji-shi, a Bachelor of Arts from Datong University. Other faculty, such as Liu Zhi-gen, a Bachelor of Arts from Tsinghua University, Min Kui-yi, a Bachelor of Science from National Zhejiang University, Hu Xiang-wen, an assistant teacher from National Business College, and Chen Meng-qiu, a Bachelor of Commerce from Guanghua University, have all been reappointed. Several newly hired faculty and staff members are also graduates of universities in China and abroad. The school opened on the 1st, with fee payment and registration from the 3rd to the 5th, and classes officially beginning on the 6th.

Shanghai Drama and Film Institute The Shanghai Drama and Film Institute on Jiangwan Road Gongyuan Fang in this city, which has been registered with the Municipal Bureau of Education, is holding its second enrollment. In addition to applicants in Shanghai, recruitment offices have been set up in major provinces and cities throughout the country, and applications for prospectuses are very enthusiastic. The institute has added the dramatist Zuo Ming as a full-time professor and is preparing to publish a monthly magazine, "Drama and Film."

Children's Educational Novel *Little Boy* (One)(Six)(Nine)

— Translated by Zheng Xiao-cang

"Bisey was sentenced to death. He petitioned the king to allow him to return home to visit his parents, promising to return to receive his punishment by a certain date. His close friend, Tan Meng, volunteered to be held hostage in his place. The king then imprisoned Tan Meng and allowed Bisey to go home. As the appointed date approached, Bisey had not yet returned, and Tan Meng was bound and taken to the execution ground to take his place. Just as the execution was about to begin, Bisey arrived in the wind and rain. The king, though tyrannical, was moved by their righteousness and released them both." (Note)

The children were deeply impressed by this immortal story, because they had just been deeply moved by the righteousness of a pair of young friends. Lying is not appropriate, but in order to repay a confidant, risking disgrace and calmly enduring humiliation for others—this great courage, this noble righteousness, made Dunn a hero they admired. Honesty and integrity have now gained a new meaning. A good name is more precious than wealth. Once lost, no amount of money can redeem it; and mutual trust can make life peaceful and happy, which nothing else can compare to.

Tao Mo happily resumed his original "company" name. Nai De was even more loyal to Dunn. The children all thought of ways to make up for their past suspicions and contempt for the two of them. Mrs. Shu was overjoyed to see her group of children. Mr. Pei praised the immortal deeds of his pair of young righteous friends without tiring.

(Note) Damon and Pyrhias. The king was Dionysus (the original text only lists the names of the two people, the translation supplements the story). The story of Jing Ke and Fan Yuqi in our country is also somewhat similar. (End of chapter)

Financial Market: Silver Prices Decline, Stimulating Buying Sentiment, Standard Gold Rises 2.2 Yuan

Fluctuations of Only 2.4 Yuan in One Day. Transaction Volume Also Only Slightly Over 6,000 Taels

The gold market yesterday saw a slight increase in buying sentiment due to the decline in silver prices. Exports to the Americas were 24,538 bales, an increase of 19,283 bales compared to 5,255 bales in the twenty-third year. Exports to ports in Asia and Africa were 9,105 bales, an increase of 886 bales compared to 8,219 bales in the twenty-third year. Total exports were 55,007 bales, an increase of 31,299 bales compared to 23,708 bales in the twenty-third year.

Last year's Shanghai Chinese tea exports, according to the report of the Tea Inspection Department of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, were 13,215.19 metric tons of green tea, 69,318.71 dan of black tea, 68,342.92 dan of brick tea, and 14,446.09 dan of other tea, totaling 290,322.91 dan, a decrease of over 80,000 dan compared to the total in the twenty-third year. Among them, black tea saw the largest decrease, totaling over 44,000 dan, followed by brick tea, totaling over 30,000 dan. However, green tea saw a slight increase. The following table compares the figures for December of last year and the entire year with the twenty-third year:

Shen Bao Literary Weekly

Blood

— Bai

The man stood in front of the bed, spreading his hands, pleading with the woman. His eyes shone with begging light, almost crying: "If you still don't believe me, then I really want to commit suicide!"

The woman pursed her lips, smiling contemptuously: "Humph!" She turned over and went to sleep facing the bed. Her hand was scribbling randomly on a glass mirror inside the bed, asking: "Use a pistol, sleeping pills, or our kitchen knife?" She desperately suppressed her laughter because she should be angry now.

The man was struck, seeing the cold face in the mirror, he couldn't help but hold his head in his hands, grabbing his hair, making a gesture of unbearable pain. But the woman's eyes closed.

The man suddenly thought of the kitchen knife—the kitchen knife the woman mentioned. He turned his head and looked through the crack in the door to the alcove used as a kitchen. On a table lay a shiny kitchen knife, emitting a cold, icy light. He couldn't help but feel a chill all over his body and turned back.

"!..." He had not forgotten the tremulous tone he used to use on stage to express affection and sorrow, and called out softly. —But she, did not respond. The sound of breathing grew louder, making it seem like she was asleep.

The man's voice was even more miserable: "Ah!… Ah-Lan!…!"

She suddenly turned over, pulling a face: "I didn't commit suicide either, what are you yelling about!"

He was as embarrassed as a rabbit, lowering his voice: "Lan, do you really not believe me?"

"Don't believe it! Don't believe it! I won't believe it even if I die!"

Everyone was silent.

She said angrily: "A wife only needs to have three meals a day, and she has enjoyed all her rights, why should she care about someone else's lover or not?"

The man knelt in front of the bed. "Do you really believe I love her?"

She pounded the edge of the bed. "I don't care about your bullshit! Don't talk to me!"

He spoke in a softer voice: "Lan, don't worry, no matter what, I won't fall in love with her!…" He waited a moment, and then said: "Don't be suspicious, how can you avoid contact with people in social interactions?… Just believe me,… just believe me!…" He himself believed his own words, his eyes turned to the sky, his hands clasped together, as if he was swearing to others, and his chest was filled with grievances.

She just opened her mouth: "You?…"

He continued in a gentler voice: "For example, yourself, your cousin…" His heart felt a pang of bitterness. "He's so close to you, but can I doubt you?"

Her heart stirred, and her face suddenly felt a little hot, she couldn't speak for a moment. She cursed him: "Bullshit!" Then she turned to face the bed again.

He still explained to her with such a good temper: "Lan, your problem is that you are too suspicious! But you are wrong: you shouldn't suspect others first; because you should first see if I have something to do with it… Lan, you should believe me!…" He called out like a sheep.

"! "The wife sneered: "Asking me to trust you is harder than asking me to believe I'm dead!" She slapped the side of the bed: "I'm telling you: I want to sleep, don't talk to me anymore!" She wrapped the quilt around herself and fell towards the inside.

The man stood blankly in front of the bed.

He thought, looking for a way to prove his loyalty.

The kitchen knife in the kitchen emitted a cold, icy light, quietly staring at him. He couldn't help but think of his own words, and he felt his hair stand on end. He hardened his heart, rushed into the kitchen, and grabbed the kitchen knife.

It's a pity that this kitchen knife is too clumsy in style: the handle is so short, the blade has no point, and it is square, just like a shovel! This made him miss the dagger that the Syrian boy used to commit suicide in the Salome on stage: it had a beautifully decorated handle and a cone-shaped blade. Holding it against the chest, it was a kind of heroic spirit! He couldn't help but loosen his hand, and the kitchen knife fell to the ground with a "slap". He walked out of the alcove in despair. He sighed long and dejectedly.

But he could not just settle down in his heart. He was still looking everywhere for things that could be used. Good, a pair of scissors was shining under the dressing table. He grabbed it. —At the same time, he looked back at her on the bed, she was still sleeping with her face turned inward. —Turning around, he pulled out the scissors and looked at them for a while. He was thinking: "Oh, I remember she bought this from the Sincere Company to trim her nails!" This is an American product, the style is very beautiful, it is nickel-plated on the outside, shining brightly. Holding it upside down in his hand, with the scissor head facing inward, it actually looked like a dagger!

He tried to stab himself in the throat. But the one on the bed was still sleeping with her face turned inward, without any sound.

He stood there for a while, feeling that although the scissors were beautiful, they were not sharp. At most, this thing would make people bleed painfully, but it could not satisfy his demands. He sighed again.

But he still couldn't feel at ease. —So he searched his body for something to use, and finally found a fleshy part on the side of his thigh. —The reason why he specially looked for this place was not because it was not important; but because he felt that: first, this place was very easy to reach; second, this kind of thing was not deliberately showing off to people, not letting people see it showed that it came from the heart. —So, he started; he carefully cut his left leg, but the muscle was a little elastic and slipped. He hated that the scissors were not sharp enough, so he immediately pinched the flesh hard and cut it. Hey, immediately a triangular scar appeared!

He watched the wound in pain, but no blood flowed out, he was disappointed. The scissors fell to the ground with a "snap".

But half a minute later, a trace of bright red blood flowed out of the wound. Although it was such a thin strand, he seemed to see a torrent of blood, staring in shock, without even wiping it off, letting it flow longer and longer.

So: "Ah! Blood…" he shouted:

He saw her turn her body further inside, and fall asleep again. And in that mirror, a smiling face of contempt appeared. —It was like a basin of cold water was poured on his heart, he was stunned.

After a while of silence, the man slumped into a chair in despair. That night, he was so angry that he couldn't fall asleep.

The one on the bed didn't sleep either, she was thinking: what method to use to retaliate against him.

Frontier Clouds

— Yingzi

The wind, like a wild beast freed from its cage, was howling in the desert plains and frontier cities, striking coldly not only people's faces and bodies but also their hearts. As the weather turned cold and harsh, people, like hibernating soft-bodied animals, stopped moving. The only ones left on the streets were wandering people calling out for grandfathers and grandmothers. Was it safe to stay at home? Perhaps! Safe in the sense that you could avoid going out and freezing your body, hands, and feet, or even lying down without realizing it. But what loomed large in everyone's mind was that question mark of insecurity: "When will 'they' come?" Looking up at the sky, the sky was a vast expanse of blue, like a boundless deep sea. Early in the morning, you could still hear the cawing of crows in flocks and the humming of pigeons released by wild children with "bamboo tubes" attached to them, which was very loud in the fresh air.

The local newspapers, like toy dolls wearing the same mask, printed rigid government orders, mostly the talks of Mongolian dignitaries. The frontier clouds seemed to be sunny days on these pages. Occasionally, there were also reports of stable news. But even so, it was revealed that "they" were already deploying, and perhaps a thunderbolt would strike in the cold weather of winter, shaking the people trapped in the cold cellar of body and mind.

Secretly, people would ask each other when they met: "! What's happening? Are they coming? Alas! Alas! Surely there's still the Lunar New Year to get through!" In secret, with the power of "they", [some people] became active, doing the same old things. The Rising Sun flag flew high in a corner of the city, symbolizing the success of these people.

What should we do?

An airplane dragging a red ball tail flew over the blue sky as usual, so low that you could see who was sitting in the plane. People didn't know where these planes came from or where they were going, they just muttered: "Won't they drop eggs?"

With the increasing power of [some people], people cast another dark shadow deep in their hearts, recalling memories from hundreds of years ago: "Ah! Soldiers are cruel!" The shadow of Genghis Khan's massacres, like a whip, struck fear into people's hearts.

"The barbarian hordes move south to graze their horses." The literate people thought in their hearts: "That day is coming soon!"

The families of people from outside were slowly moving back home. Where should the people of the frontier move? Let's wait! Living one day at a time, the people of the frontier are true "live for today" people.

The frontier clouds are gradually changing color! The Fiery Mountain is covered with snowflakes, and everything is quietly waiting for that clap of thunder!

Untitled

— Qi Fu

"We're going out to give a speech today," my nephew told me excitedly when he came back very late at night.

"Did you blush?" I asked with a smile. "Did anyone listen?"

"Yes, this is my first time giving a speech. I not only blushed, but my voice also trembled a little. But it will be fine after giving a few speeches. There were several hundred people listening, and some people even asked us to give the speech."

When my nephew reported to me with the enthusiasm and pride of youth, I, who have been living in memories lately, deeply felt that I was old.

When the May Fourth Movement swept in, I, with the same youthful enthusiasm and pride, chased after the waves. When the blood-curdling cries of "March 8th" came, I also excitedly followed my classmates to give maiden propaganda speeches. In the ranks of the May 30th Movement, I began to understand the greatness of the masses and began to gain a sense of "unity of purpose." The bloodstains splashed on my body on "June 23rd" were even more like the brand of an initiate, imprinted on my life. Later, I also held my breath under thousands of flags and stood on end among the thunderous shouts, but that was no longer in China.

All of this has now become a trace of history. Youth has left me behind, and the sound of the great waves has gradually faded away, far away.

In a steady and unobtrusive manner, the "September 18th" Incident and the "January 28th" Incident passed through a few unstable years. Even the corpses of the "May Fourth" and "March 8th" eras have finally been resurrected, and have been resurrected with a new and more terrifying face. However, in front of them, blood is still flowing, and blood is still first smeared on the ancient city that is like a tomb with a tragic history, and the blood is still the blood of the enthusiastic and proud youth—even though it is the second generation of youth.

Although scholars' rebellion takes three years to fail, the students who interfere in politics, because they are good at slander, have been thorns in the back of the rulers since ancient times. They will not be happy until they are pulled out. The imprisoned college students at the end of the Eastern Han Dynasty and the Donglin Fushe who were killed in the late Ming Dynasty were all destined for the same fate. Yes, in the mouths of the older generation, behaviors such as boycotting classes and parades are not mischievous pranks of children, but also reckless actions that are not content with their own duties. —Even though some of them personally did such heinous things, but, this is one time and that is another! —However, in their hearts, they never believe that this is a simple malicious prank, but a vortex that can stir the water mill of history. In France in 1789, the Parisian masses who destroyed the Bastille prison and the hungry women who forced Louis XVI to return to Paris from Versailles, were not they also seen as childish troublemakers in the eyes of the nobles at the time, and even in the writings of some historians? In the colony, wouldn't such mass truancy have almost the same serious impact?

Of course, great movements are not accomplished by this, but great movements often begin with this.

Only the individual is old, but the history of the entire human society is constantly renewed and advanced with the vitality of youth.

I Still Have One Eye

— Zhang Chunqiao

Arise, you enslaved ones filled with anger!

Burn, you compressed layers of coal!

Roar, my beloved brothers!

Please sit here for a moment,

Don't say this place is too terribly dim,

The dirty soil will stain your clothes,

And the squinting dust.

Yes, this is a large temple,

Living here is like being in a tomb,

The owl cries a string of sorrow,

The sorrowful song accompanies the statue,

The withered old cypress is silent,

The wings of the big wind cannot fan back its life.

But, you have to know there are times,

This place is as turbulent as the seaside,

That's a temple fair or some memorial,

People hold feasts here,

I clearly know this place,

Like knowing I only have one eye left.

(If you don't believe me,

Strike a match and take a look—

One spitting out bright light,

The other has lost its flame.)

Speaking of which, it's been a long time,

A bitterly cold winter,

Our army was stationed in Shanghai,

A wide road separating two worlds,

On one side, the angry us,

Armed enemies standing opposite.

Gun barrels aimed at the enemy,

Hearts leaping like flames,

As long as a shout,

Bombs melted the ice.

The winter streets were especially desolate,

Towering houses flashing ghostly shadows,

Gunshots rang out on the dark horizon,

Qiujiang Road, Baoshan Road, became torches,

In an instant, the sky was burning red,

Arise, you enslaved ones filled with anger!

Burn, you compressed layers of coal!

We are like a herd of crazy beasts,

Blood splashes wake up the enemy's dreams!

What cannot be forgotten are those brothers,

Chain of love, grasped until hands hurt,

They are workers, farmers, students,

We are soldiers!

Holding up guns, the sound rings in our ears:

"Charge! Defend our brothers!"

But I was injured, lost an eye,

We were confined to the hospital,

Every heart tied to the battlefield.

"Don't ask, don't read the newspaper,

Don't think about those things."

The enemy's plane rattled,

We were carried to the rear again.

Later, I heard, "Ceasefire!"

What the heck!

This is clearly a lie,

How could we fail,

We have countless brothers!

From then on, I was blind, blind in one eye,

Left the hospital,

Lived in this ancient temple.

From morning to night, from night to morning,

I hope one day,

The enemy will be driven out of the country,

Every day I wander on the old battlefield,

A stretch of ruined houses, lying,

Like a clumsy old bear.

Sloping stone pillars, pieces of white bones,

Everything is still like yesterday.

My brother is buried here,

Wang Desheng is buried here,

Zhang Jinzhong is also buried here.

One day, this family started to dig,

That family started construction again.

Today, it has restored its past state,

Today, there are no angry gunshots!

Arise, you enslaved ones filled with anger!

Burn, you compressed layers of coal!

Roar, my beloved brothers!

Although I only have one eye left,

I can see the world clearly,

Only by lighting torches,

The iron chain will not loosen!

Staring with this eye,

I sing loudly for a bright day!

The Strange Carpenter

— Ouyang Shan

It doesn't need proof that many people waste their lives through their compromises, selfishness, and laziness. But many others are wasted by life. Life is created by humanity -- based on reason, so it is wonderful. But is it really so? When it is entangled in a deceptive web and falls straight into the pit of sin, it will drag down countless people along with it... Isn't reason ugly, paradoxical, and a shameful mistake? ...

The strange Shen Jia was a young, gentle, and skillful carpenter. -- Yes, everyone knew that there was such a carpenter in Guanfu Lane. His cheekbones and teeth protruded outward, his face was long and small, his short black hair stood up on his head like a large brush, his eyes were not very bright, covered with coarse red blood vessels. He was strong, cheerful, unmarried, and passionately loved other people's children.

He said:

"Making chairs and tables -- that doesn't count as being a carpenter! Carving vase stands and planing gunstocks are the most shameless things to do!"

His boss, Wang Fulai, replied:

"That's not how it works. Everyone who follows my orders is a carpenter! What -- 'I don't like to do this, I can't do that,' are clearly wrong. My words are right."

Wang Fulai was a famous, wealthy local who gambled on pigeon lotteries and was very good at exploiting his employees.

Shen Jia was one of the most inattentive and unmotivated employees. He yawned long and surprisingly in front of Wang Fulai, as if he hadn't had a good night's sleep in years. He fell asleep on the planing bench, almost forcing his boss to kick him awake with his cloth shoe. "Aren't you planning to keep working here?"

"Can't you give me a little raise?" he replied, as if Wang Fulai had done something very wrong to him and he had already generously forgiven him, only to honestly continue out of embarrassment: "I know you'll eventually fire me. But if you really do that, you know you'll starve me to death."

Wang Fulai gave him an extra two cents in wages every day. He was obeying a saying: "Good things aren't cheap, cheap things aren't good." Shen Jia's cheekbones protruded even further and were bright red, shining with oil, indicating his happiness.

But in less than two months, he relapsed into laziness and depression.

His head drooped thoughtfully, his upper and lower lips twisted and cracked -- everyone believed it was because they had tried so hard to contain those teeth, and that was the result.

"You see, I'm just not like this kind of person. -- Isn't it inexcusable to be unfair to the boss?"

He roared, telling his spiritual phenomena to his uncle, Shen Zezhi. Shen Zezhi was a hopeless opium addict, with a pale gray face, his shoulders always shrugging as if cold, and his lips large and everted.

"Okay, let me see what kind of person you are."

He wandered silently around the room, picked up clothes, teacups, looked at them meticulously, smelled them, and then after a dozen minutes, he slowly asked his nephew, Shen Jia:

"Now, give me some money." Only when he received invitations and orders from roommates or neighbors was he happy and enthusiastic, completely regaining the vitality of youth.

He took wood, ash oil, paint, trim, and other kinds of furniture supplies from the store home without letting Wang Fulai know. It was painful for him to do this. He did it for a certain pleasure that he couldn't get otherwise, and he could also estimate how much those materials were worth under the boss's plan.

He made many cabinets, square chairs, chicken coops, low stools, and washstands for others without receiving any payment. He also often responded to their calls to repair things like wardrobes, Eight Immortals tables, planks, and ancestral shrines. Once he even completely repainted a pair of brown door panels.

Sometimes they treated him to two hundred cash worth of double-distilled liquor.

"Really -- how can you live like this?"

"I didn't do it for you. I did it for myself."

He replied to everyone this way.

His ingenious ideas and true ability were expressed in the toys he tried to make, and some things that looked like toys but couldn't be designated for any use. This young carpenter in his twenties used saws, planes, chisels, lathes, and hammers -- these clumsy tools -- to make some things that were indeed very interesting.

The small room was so dark that even in the daytime, it needed to be lit. It was filled with the results of his work. Among them were several things he truly liked: a large wooden plate with various small creatures made of wood -- people, cows, dogs, horses; according to his wishes, he could change the positions of each, one chasing after another, or leading, biting, or wrestling. Two people carved from a piece of wood, a man and a woman, their heads and limbs were movable, so they could hug each other intimately, or fight each other fiercely. A snow-white goose with a long neck and high bun, the skin layer could be opened, inside there were colored viscera -- this was imitated from some kind of cross-sectional animal specimen displayed in the window of a bookstore on Shuangmen Bottom Street. On the wall was a lion dance picture, only partially completed, drawn first with ink, and then made of colored wooden strips, pieces, and iron pieces, broken glass. -- After finishing work at the store, he would work and play silently in the room.

He gave even his most beloved things as gifts to some children, those who were familiar with him or unrelated, even just passers-by.

Rough, crude, but abundant talent, this carpenter found this way to consume it.

His opium-smoking uncle, Shen Zezhi, came and argued with him for two hours. He asked Shen Jia to give him some toys to exchange for money, but Shen Jia sternly refused.

Shen Zezhi brought the boss, Wang Fulai, to his nephew's room. That was a few days later. Wang Fulai howled there like a wounded wild boar, cried tears, and destroyed all the objects there -- whether they belonged to him or not. ...

Two months after being fired, the unlucky carpenter Shen Jia went to work as a laborer in a small tin mining company in Guangxi.

On Issues of New Poetry Creation

— Lei Shiyu

Recently, the various issues concerning new poetry seem to have been hotly debated in some newspapers, but up to now, no one has made a systematic poetic theory that is concrete and correct on the issues of new poetry creation. Many poetry writers or poets, because of scattered opinions, do not know who is right and who is wrong, and are still doubting the goal of creation and creative activities. In fact, poetry is like novels (of course, different in form and technical expression) and cannot be used as a mechanical form as an unchanging model to call people to imitate. It is nothing more than a literary tool that reflects the consciousness of the era and the reality of society. The era and society are not an egg, so the elements of poetry cannot be analyzed into egg yolk ( ), egg white ( ), eggshell, etc. in certain quantities. Just taking form as an example, the ancient ballad type, the feudal rhythmic type, the capitalist free verse type, and the emerging non-rhythmic type can show how the process of poetry development is changing, just like the changes in history.

Reality is undoubtedly changing, but it is not simply, regularly, and nakedly taken into the laboratory like dissecting a rabbit or analyzing a cup of water's composition. Because just looking at the superficial phenomena and not grasping or deeply understanding the essence of reality containing diversity and complex relationships, it is easy to distort reality. (Of course, there are also people who deliberately distort reality, because exposing the essence of reality is equal to exposing the ugliness and unfortunate fate of his own class.) Therefore, as a progressive poet, attempting to grasp or promote the inevitable trend of history and expressing one's own not "pure" emotions reflected from reality, the correct understanding of the world view, and the tempering of ideology are very necessary. But in order to vividly represent living reality in an artistic image, or to strengthen the emotional impact on the masses, the use of form and technique cannot be ignored.

Precisely because the real society is not an unhatched egg (even such an egg changes, but there is no development), the rhythmic types such as jue, lv, and ancient have entered the grave with our queue poets, and the "Hu Shi style" of the gentry bourgeoisie can only exist in the pockets of a few people in suits (but people who wear suits may not all be happy to put the "Hu Shi style" in their pockets), because we now need more concrete, more real, more tragic, and more leaping expressions. At present, how to express it effectively and how to best obtain the method of expression is a topic worthy and urgent discussion.

The masses of China, who are caught in the most miserable life and the most cruel oppression, and whose cultural education is the lowest or non-existent, and all the badge-wearing or non-badge-wearing traitors who shamelessly hold the crutches of imperialism to whip, slaughter, and enslave the masses... are precisely the objects we want to express. At the same time, because we are standing in the layer of the masses, as singers of the masses, we cannot ignore and must study and adapt to the vision and hearing of the masses and pull it blindly.

However, the development of new poetry in the past year or two has been too pessimistic. Not only is there not a single poetry magazine that can be regarded as representative, but there is not even a more progressive one that is regularly published. Even some of the poetry works published in newspapers and literary magazines are mostly disappointing. This does not mean that there are no progressive poets writing poetry. I believe that many useful works have been trampled on. At the same time, because there is no encouragement and opportunity to publish, it affects the pessimism and laziness of many poetry writers. Some poets with a little reputation do not turn to individual activities, do not excavate new poets for the development of the poetry world, and cannot produce good poems if they are separated from the activities of the masses. Therefore, the future and way out of the development of new poetry are becoming increasingly bleak.

However, I do not deny the devastation and embarrassment of politics and economics. In fact, precisely because of this, we must strengthen the struggle more technically and more arduously.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Germany's Second Bomb

— Xing An

Since Germany abandoned the Treaty of Versailles and implemented rearmament, it has been like a tiger released from its cage, looking down on everything, causing all European countries to be on guard. But Germany's rearmament was just the first bomb thrown to the world. Now Germany's second bomb is about to explode. Hitler is preparing to demand the return of old colonies and restore armed forces in the Rhineland region. Hitler plans to hold a referendum in April, submitting two questions to the citizens for approval. The questions are: (1) Do the German people need colonies? (2) Is the restoration of armed forces in the Rhineland region consistent with Germany's dignity? This kind of referendum is enough to illustrate Germany's future direction.

In recent years, Germany has never forgotten its previous old colonies. Hitler has made blatant expressions in his speeches in various countries, saying that Germany is unwilling to give up its old colonies forever. Recently, he lectured to students at the National Socialist Party University in Müllre, saying that European countries have the right to colonize overseas, and Germany is now very strong, does not need League of Nations aid, and does not need treaties or alliances. Colonies are obtained by strong power. Germany's determination to strive for colonies can be seen from this. Regarding this request, the Japanese authorities recently declared that there is no reason to return the territories administered by Japan to Germany. I wonder what method Hitler will adopt in the future to demand the return of old colonies. Is it necessary to use strong power to achieve its goal?

As for restoring armed forces in the Rhineland region, according to recent reports from France, Germany has secretly laid out an "air Hindenburg Line" in the area, preparing for a second invasion of France. It is also said that all the most modern airports in the area have underground aircraft shelters that defend against bombs, each room can accommodate a hundred aircraft. The line stretches from the North Sea to the Swiss border. There is also a second line, which is also a similar aircraft field, the location of which is suitable for providing strategic retreat for the first line. Regarding the re-establishment of defenses in the demilitarized zone of the Rhineland, Germany not only does not deny it, but has also tried its best to promote it. Now this issue has attracted the attention of France. French Foreign Minister Flandin, who participated in the funeral of the late British monarch, has discussed with British Foreign Secretary Eden how to deal with Germany. Although Britain believes that Germany's move does not pose an immediate danger, it is prepared to assist France in its policy of preparing for emergencies. In addition, Belgium and France are closely dependent on each other, and also expressed sympathy for France's policy. It was also decided to set up defense works along the Muse River, from Liege, which is adjacent to Germany, to the border of France. On the Italian side, former French Prime Minister Laval also contacted him once before resigning. The Italian authorities immediately declared that if Germany violates the terms of the peace treaty, Italy's military strength is sufficient to deal with the incident. As such, the European situation is now in a tense state, and the future is difficult to be optimistic about.

Hitler is determined to build the Third Germany, and it has been three years since he came to power. Although Germany itself is becoming increasingly strong, world peace has been greatly threatened.

On New Year Pictures

— Hua Mu

During the Lunar New Year, in addition to gathering family members and enjoying family life, people generally have a more important meaning, which is that everyone, in addition to having fun, also wants an auspicious sign to seek happiness and the safety of livestock for the year. It is very clear just to look at the red paper couplets pasted on the gates and rooms of every household. In addition, the various New Year pictures sold in the painting stalls can also be seen from the colors and intentions of the paintings. Mr. Zhitang is very good at talking about New Year pictures. He once used a sarcastic feeling to say that most of these New Year pictures with this kind of meaning are "apotropaic paintings" that carry morality and are a manifestation of the outdated ideas of the literati. Mr. Zhitang's words naturally came from his own feelings, and he did not necessarily sincerely ridicule the simple-minded rural people whose thoughts and lives were very simple. The villagers work hard all year round, and it is not easy to have porridge to drink for two meals a day. They rely on the customs inherited from thousands of years to be able to relax for a few days in the New Year. What they expect is of course to hope that the days will pass more smoothly in the future, that's all.

There is also a Mr. Sun Fuxi who has also written articles on New Year pictures, which are also very interesting. He was originally a painter, and he naturally has his own unique insights when talking about New Year pictures with the feelings of a painter. However, regardless of whether these New Year pictures are elegant art paintings or "apotropaic paintings" that carry morality, they are indeed fresh decorations for the folk Lunar New Year. As for not forgetting to pray for blessings in addition to having fun, the intentions are extremely difficult. The demand for life is originally endowed by human instinct, and the New Year pictures that carry morality are also a kind of call for and expression of the folk's demand for survival. Even if the thoughts are outdated, the original motivation is undeniable.

Speaking of New Year pictures in my hometown, they are not common. Perhaps the reason for this is that the people in my hometown lack a talent for creating their own popular art. For example, in the way of singing operas, the people in my hometown do not have enough scripts for themselves to sing and perform. During the Lunar New Year, the area around the South Gate of the county town is a painting market, but these paintings are completely different from the New Year pictures commonly referred to. They are all beauty paintings and landscape ink paintings that are贩回来from Shanghai. The villagers cannot afford large mirror screen paintings, so they have to seek cheap and good-looking ones, buy one or two and hang them on the walls of their rooms, which is also a kind of fresh wall decoration. It seems that they can appreciate elegant art quite well. However, in terms of seeking auspiciousness, people still have to paste spring couplets during the New Year, and they are pasted in a big and elaborate way. Zhong Kui images are also pasted on the two large door panels, saying that this Zhong Kui portrait is the real New Year picture of the people in my hometown, because there is really no other kind to say besides this. As for the mouse marrying a daughter, there is only a verbal description, and no one is going to paint it for people to see what the scene is like.

When I was a child, although I found the beauty paintings in the painting stalls to be colorful and very beautiful, I could only occasionally stand in front of them and take a look, and I couldn't afford to buy them. Sometimes the ones bought by the adults were hung on the wall early. What is worth mentioning is the woodcut print of the Kitchen God riding a white horse that was挟in the memorial tablet when送灶on the twenty-third day of the twelfth lunar month. There was a wealth-bringing boy following behind. The paper was extremely rough, and the engraving was often blurred and untrue. However, at that time, I already felt it was extremely precious, and I often secretly揭it down and hid it to play with it, although my grandmother had said that without this little white horse, the Kitchen God could not go to heaven, and I could not manage so much.

Regarding New Year pictures, I will not say anything else, but I cannot help but say that the lack of toys for the children in my hometown is a kind of harm to the cultivation and enlightenment of children's interest and wisdom.

Shelter From the Cold

— Xin Ye

The sky was still only dimly lit, and there was a sound of shouting in the corridor outside; it was the warden calling the guards to get up.

It was still pitch black in the shed, although a few wisps of gray-white dawn light leaked in through the gaps in the reed mat, but it did not drive away the darkness in the shed after all.

In that crowded shed, four or five hundred poor people lay horizontally and vertically, all crowded on the spread straw like a group of piglets, and an unpleasant smell followed a burst of snoring and酝酿in the shed.

I opened my eyes in a dark corner and looked around, only to see that the bald head not far from me had been coughing and spitting phlegm all night until dawn. Those young people often woke up from their dreams and muttered to him:

"Why does such an old man still want to live in this world?"

Listening to the sounds outside, they were more noisy than just now. I knew that this group of guards had already gone "to work." Because I really couldn't sleep anymore, I supported a stiff body and crawled out of a quilt with more than a dozen holes. I looked at the guy lying at my feet, but he was still sleeping like a dead pig. I kicked him a few times vigorously, but he didn't wake up.

Last night's cold劲was really terrible. My body had not been warm all night, and the guy lying at my feet was also naughty, turning over for a while and urinating a little, which was really annoying. I will never share the quilt with him again tonight—but the rattan sticks of those guards are really unbearable.

As soon as I mentioned those guards, I got angry; they had a piece of red cloth wrapped around their arms and a rattan stick in their hands, posing like hillbillies from the Northern Grand Sword Team. In fact, they are just monkeys in official positions, and they don't come from the same background as us. Poor people, we are all poor people, why be so snobbish! Anyway, they just have a few pounds of strength and are a few years younger. If my father was ten years younger, he would rather starve to death than come to this hellish place to suffer.

According to my temper, I really want to twist these little turtles and beat them up to teach them a lesson so that I can let out a breath of stink, but it won't work. There are many of them, and the wardens will kick me out.

Thinking about it, I needed to urinate, so I touched the dark wall and stood up, straddling over one person lying down. Sometimes I stepped on their bodies and had to let them curse a few words:

"You're going to die, are you blind?" I can't ignore them.

The shed gradually brightened up, and the footsteps under the eaves began to get busy. One by one, the companions lying on the straw also sat up.

"Go wash your face!" The jailer-like guard shouted, sticking his head in the door, so everyone staggered and swarmed into a courtyard.

Under the reed shed in the middle of the courtyard, there were three wooden buckets of hot water. Many people rushed to wash their faces. The young and strong squeezed in front, while the old, weak, and children were轧落behind. By the time they had all washed, it was our turn, the elderly. Therefore, every time I went to wash, the water had turned into mud, and the cloth was black. It was cold and dirty, and I really didn't want to say it. However, I couldn't help but wash it, or the managing gentlemen would scold me for not understanding hygiene.

After washing our faces, it was time for breakfast; everyone gathered under the porch waiting, and on each gray-green face, there was a kind of hunger shining!

As usual, breakfast in the first shed was eaten first—it was always like this—at this time, a gust of congee fragrance followed the northwest wind, making us all gulp and swallow saliva as we stood there; it felt as if there were small insects crawling in our throats, which made us feel very uncomfortable. I only hoped that the congee would be sent over soon so that we could fill the emptiness in our stomachs.

After each of the six large wooden buckets of congee was sent to us, it would be抢得精光in a few minutes. Although it was just salted radish and thin rice porridge, it was even more rare than white rice and a big wine banquet when we ate it.

After eating breakfast, we still went to the籩子里to lie down or sit and wait for lunch.

River Dredging

— Zhang Yan

In winter, when the tides are low, the key point of this official road—under the drawbridge outside the city—is often crowded with boats coming and going. The semi-dried up river water allows for a clear view of the silt and stones at the bottom of the river; while the riverbanks along both sides, accumulated with years of dumped garbage, make the river channel appear even narrower. Every day around noon, boats from Sifen Township to the county seat, or from the county seat to the surrounding villages, must pass through this crucial center, under the drawbridge; but the shallow and narrow river channel blocks them. If the boats coming from behind refuse to give way, everyone insists on going head-to-head, and often the boats cannot move an inch. The noisy arguments then attract the attention of pedestrians on the drawbridge.

This situation reached the ears of the gentry elders, and they informally discussed this matter at a dinner table. Originally, this official road was scheduled to have the river dredged every five years, presided over by the elder of the year (naturally also one of the gentry elders), who would formally convene a meeting. After everyone agreed, donation books would be distributed door-to-door to collect money. The leading gentry elders would have tens of dollars listed next to their names on the first page, making it embarrassing for larger shops and middle-to-upper-class people to write down amounts that were too small. Thus, each elder in charge could earn a special fee on this official road to spend on prostitutes.

However, it was not yet the scheduled time for the five-year dredging. As a result of the informal negotiation, everyone ostensibly expounded on grand arguments under the major themes of "facilitating transportation and maintaining commerce." The county magistrate's uncle, whom everyone called Master Zhong, and who was also the host of this "dinner table" gathering, said with a smile and seriousness that the market was currently sluggish, and it was already difficult to ask businesses to donate money once every five years. Only two years had passed since the last dredging. Although they knew the river's traffic had a close relationship with their business, it might not be easy to ask businesses to share this unexpected dredging donation at the end of the year? Finally, he got to the point, suggesting he try to obtain a sum of public funds from the county, and that the gentry elders also donate a little more. "This is doing a good deed!" Master Zhong smiled like a heron.

This proposal won much applause and flattering words at the "dinner table." Master Zhong was very pleased with his handling of this matter. Because if he went to the county to obtain public funds, he could naturally preside over this extra dredging, and a sum of "Tang Pool" money would surely be in his hands. But the gentry elders were no more foolish than Master Zhong. Everyone wanted to compete with all their might to be the host of this dredging. However, none of them had the connections to obtain public funds from the county. Therefore, on one hand, they agreed with Master Zhong's proposal, letting him focus on obtaining public funds. After leaving Master Zhong's house, they formed a group and held another meeting. Their defensive method was to contact the foremen of private construction teams first, setting a trap for Master Zhong to fall into, and then they would jointly sign their names

Page 18

to start dredging the river.

Relying on his nephew's (county magistrate) influence, the public funds were successfully obtained. Master Zhong naturally prepared another banquet to entertain the gentry elders. At the banquet, Master Zhong used diplomatic tactics to win them over. On the surface, everyone supported Master Zhong as the host of this dredging. The next day, a tender notice was posted in the city.

As the end of the year approached, the official river was a crucial thoroughfare. Master Zhong advocated for damming the river first. The tender could be concluded and construction could start immediately after three days. However, after the second three-day period passed, there were still no bids. The county immediately received a joint official letter from various businesses, which was naturally unfavorable to Master Zhong. Although Master Zhong ran to the county magistrate's house several times, the gentry elders still came to handle the dredging matters themselves.

When the river dredging started on the first day, the gentry elders all came to the city early in the morning to watch. Their smiles were so full under the sunlight, although some still secretly thought of ways to reduce their contributions, so that they could earn a little extra money for themselves.

Special Article

A Visit to Chiba Shoyu Business in Japan (6)

— (Ye Xiyuan)

Yamasa Shoyu Company is located in Choshi Town, in the northeast of Chiba Prefecture. It is famous in Japan for brewing Yamasa soy sauce. Its capital is ten million yen, its total land area is 65,000 tsubo, its total building area is 35,000 tsubo, its annual output is 250,000 koku, it has 150 office employees, and 1,700 workers. It has three brewing factories, all in Choshi Town, Chiba Prefecture. Except for the first factory, which is an old-style factory building, the second and third factories are newly built and can compete with Noda's 17th factory. Its market covers not only Japan, Korea, and Manchuria, but also Europe and America.

Choshi Shoyu Co., Ltd. is located in Choshi Town, Chiba Prefecture. It is considered a relatively latecomer in the Japanese soy sauce brewing industry. It has a capital of five million yen and an annual soy sauce production of more than 150,000 koku. It has five brewing factories. Its fifth factory is the newest building. When we visited, it was not yet completed and required more than one million yen in construction costs. Although the scale is smaller than Noda and Yamasa, its organizational soundness, management innovation, and business efforts are probably above Noda and Yamasa. Its managing director, Mr. Hamaguchi Rinzo, is young, handsome, and ambitious, and he is greatly admired by us.

Broadcasting

Radio Script for a Play by Performers' Broadcasting Association

Temptation (Written by Liu Yawei) (3)

Little Lu: What did they say?

Eldest Brother: They said that the flood came very quickly, submerging seven or eight villages in one night. They originally lived on the border of Shang County. Now their homes have all been flooded, so they fled here overnight yesterday.

A Qiao: (Surprised) Oh dear! We are on the border of this county, aren't we very dangerous?

Eldest Brother: If it weren't dangerous, why would I be worried? Little Lu: So what do we do? Let's run away quickly!

Eldest Brother: Run away? Where to? Running is starving to death! Not running is drowning to death! Either way it's death!

A Qiao: Isn't there disaster relief coming to distribute grain? Besides, we still have half a bucket of rice!

Eldest Brother: That's right, but when will they come to distribute it? Not to mention the money donated, even if it's all distributed, how much is enough for several counties of people? You'll definitely be squeezed! Will you have a share? As for this mere half bucket of rice, if it can support our family, would you not help others when they are starving to death? In that case, isn't danger coming immediately?

Little Lu: Then why are those relief people like that?

Eldest Brother: For the sake of face, they have to pretend to make a trip to maintain face. As for their conscience, whether it has been eaten by dogs, I don't know.

A Qiao: Then why is that? Don't they also have human hearts made of flesh?

Eldest Brother: (Smiling) Because they themselves need to live better lives! What does it matter to them whether you starve to death!

Old Fifth: (Anxiously) Damn it, they only know how to eat their fill and collect rent. They don't even repair the embankments when they break. If the flood really comes, won't they also drown or flee?

Eldest Brother: They got the news long ago that the embankments wouldn't be repaired. Don't they know the danger themselves? Let me tell you, they won't be among those who drown!

Little Lu: So, what do you say we should do? Should we run away first?

Eldest Brother: Didn't I tell you? Running is death, not running is also death!

A Qiao: What can we do? Only death awaits. (About to cry)

Film

"Broken Dreams of Spring" Opens in Paris

The film "Broken Dreams of Spring," which won the top prize at the 3rd film festival held in Italy last year, is MGM's supreme structure. The film is based on Tolstoy's famous Russian work, and is a great achievement of Greta Garbo and Frederic March's first joint performance, as well as the six major stars such as Basil Rathbone, the child star of "David Copperfield," breaking New York's box office record in six years. From today on, it will be shown at the Paris Theater on Avenue Joffre. Those who want to appreciate Garbo's work, please do not miss it.

Yuan Meiyun Shaves Her Head to Be a Man

A surprising piece of news is that Yuan Meiyun held a head-shaving ceremony last night. However, this was not a head-shaving ceremony at the time of the baby's full moon, nor was it a head-shaving ceremony for becoming a nun, but a head-shaving ceremony in which a woman turned into a man in the movie "Incarnation Girl" directed by Fang Peilin and produced by Yihua Company. In the "click" of the camera sound and the "clack-clack" of the barber Mou Li's scissors, it was as if her heart was being cut, and it was obvious that her two watery eyes were filled with glittering teardrops. She stared blankly at the long black hair scattered on the ground, but her expression was not sad. Instead, she seemed to have infinite pleasure in her heart.

Yes, why did Yuan Meiyun have to cut off her hair? What kind of role does she play in "Incarnation Girl"? This mysterious and subtle mystery can only be answered by everyone themselves from "Incarnation Girl".

Lianhua's New Film "Wild Geese Over the Empty River"

— Jin Cheng Screening Today

The Experimental Theater Group Revives and Prepares for its Second Performance

The Experimental Theater Group, which was born from the Experimental Performance Institute, since participating in the flood relief fundraising concert and holding its first performance of "The Miser," has been brewing the air for a second performance. The group was temporarily suspended because the central figures flew away midway. Recently, Lu Shi, Liu Yawei, Pan Gongliang, Lu Yi, etc., were responsible for preparing to realize the hope of the second performance, and with the help of Huang Jingwan, Xia Chun, and other strengths, the work was progressing smoothly. It is heard that the scripts have been selected as "Meiluo Xiang" and "The Last Prayer," and the participating authors also include Zuo Ming, Mei Xi, Zhao Manna, Liu Liying and new recruit Ma Yuandeng.

Yue Feng's New Work "Little Tiger"

Yue Feng's new work after "Wedding Night". The script is being actively written, and it will be completed soon. The title is set as "Little Tiger". It is a moral and human drama full of detective flavor. It is said that the whole play will focus on relaxation and tension, and the play needs one hundred little fat actors around the age of sixteen or seventeen.

A Major Innovation in the Yisheng Film Monthly

The Yisheng Film Monthly has been published for six issues. It has always been known for its beautiful shape and quality materials. It has a very high position in film publications. Last year, Chen Jiazhen, the editor of the magazine, suddenly suffered from hemoptysis and was plagued for a long time, which caused the publication of Yisheng to be delayed. Now, Mr. Chen's physical strength has recovered, and he is determined to reorganize and improve the content with the greatest effort. He has also decided on the future editorial policy, restoring the music special group, adding a reader's mailbox, and introducing new knowledge and new families. The material should be rich, the form should be beautiful, the compilation should be eye-catching, and the style should be unique, so as to add a different color to the Chinese publishing industry. Also, because the original address is not enough, it has now been moved to No. 457 Hankou Road. All subscriptions or letters should be sent to the new address.

New Developments in the Yuexiang Dance Research Society

The Yuexiang Dance Research Society on the upper floors of Weidaifu Silk Store on Simalu (Fourth Road) and Shilu (Stone Road), founded half a year ago, is recognized by dance fans as a good place for recreation. Wu Yinbo, the owner of Yexiang, in order to increase the dance interest of the members, has now hired young and beautiful dance partners with proficient dance skills to accompany the members to dance day and night. He has also hired several male teachers to wholeheartedly teach the most beautiful dance postures and the latest dance steps. Now he is recruiting 20 male students, with no tuition fees, and 20 female students, with tuition fees reduced by half. The learning time is from 2 pm to 7 pm every day. A special class is also set up, and the teaching time is selected by the learners themselves. Welcome to visit and register as soon as possible.
